000625gr6b Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="gr6b" obligation="normative">
<p id="_1b7a122e-1391-0f44-89ab-873c25b5a639">Any body established in accordance with paragraph <xref target="gr6a"/> above shall be open to all Member States and may take the form of:</p>

<clause id="gr6b-i" obligation="normative">
<p id="_6f76e50a-0ccd-35b3-af42-f7d2bb0b7913">a committee, being a subsidiary organ whose life expectancy is longer than the time period between two consecutive ordinary sessions of the Assembly;</p>
